 In the scriptures, Pradosh fast is the day to get the great grace of Lord Shiva, which falls on Saturday, is called Shani Pradosh fast
 is baar ye vrath 2 farvari ke din yani aaj he
 By fasting Shani Pradosh any devotee can fulfill the desire of his mind very quickly
 har maheene kii donon pakshon kii trayodashi tithi ko yah vrath kiya jaataa he
 Lord Shani is worshiped in Shani Pradosh Vrat in the evening, 45 minutes before sunset and 45 minutes after sunset
 shani pradosh vrath main bhagwaan shiv ke saath-saath shani dev kii maha krupa bhi praapt hoti he
 The side effects of Saturn's half-century Dhaiya are also overcome
 shani pradosh vrath ke din bhagwaan shiv or shani kii puja kaise karen-- shani pradosh ke din surya udai hone se pehle uthen
 - Bath and wear clean light colored clothes
 - sarson ke tel kaa choumukha diya pipal ke ped ke neeche jalaaen or ek diya shanidev ke mandir main jalaaen
 - Chant Lord Shiva's mantra all day, Namah Shivaaya, chant the heart and remain unharmed
 - shaam ke samay pradosh kaal main bhagwaan shiv ko panchamrita (doodh, dahi, ghi, shahad or shakkar) se snaan karaaen
 After this, take a bath with pure water also
 - roli, moli, chaaval, dhoop, deep se pujan karen
 What precautions and rules should be kept during Shani Pradosh fast - Take care of cleanliness in the temple and the whole house
 - saaf-suthere kapade pahanakar hi bhagwaan shiv or shani kii puja archana karen
 - Do not let any wrong thoughts come to mind in Shani Pradosh fast
 - ghar ke sabhi log aapas main sammaan purvak baat karen
 - Do not disrespect elders nor do parents disrespect during Saturn Pradosh fast
 - shani pradosh vrath main hare bhare ped-paudhon ko naa toden
 - In all the fasting laws, surrender yourself to Lord Shiva and Shani

 # In January last year, when the attack took place at the Pathankot airbase, a commando Rajesh Negi had a splinter (shrapnel) in his eye, causing him to lose his eye
 is baat ko dhyaan main rakhte hue is tarah kii paristhitiyon se nipatane ke liye NSG ne ab belistic helmet yaa phir kahen bullate pruf helmet apane body gear main shaamil kar liye hai
 By the way, this helmet looks very common but it is amazing
 iskaa frant cover or base dono 9mem kii goli tak jhel sakate hai
 This new helmet has been designed in such a way that no matter how close the range is shot, it is effective in handling it
 ye helmet vaishvik standard ko puraa karte hai
 Also, these helmets are convenient to wear and can also be fitted with communication devices
 is sambandh main enesji ke ek varisht afasar ne enditivi india ko bataaya,"goli chaahe kitni bhi nazadiiki se chalaai jaae lekin agar kisi jawan ne ye helmet pahan rakhaa hoga to uske sir par koi chot nahin lagegi
 There are no nuts in this helmet
 iskaa vazan dhai kilo kaa he
 " unke mutabiq kisi bhi aatank rodhi oparation main commando kaa body gear qareeb 28 kilo kaa hota he
 Now two more kilograms will be added to it
 is maamle main is tarah ke aatank rodhi oparation se jude ek commando kaa kahana he,"yah bahut zaruri he kii aapkaa sir surakshit rahe
 When the bullet is moving, it can hit anywhere
 pehle ham apana sir bachaate rahete the lekin ab is helmet se hamaari suraksha bhi bad gai he
 " sabase acchhee baat ye he ki ise bharat main hi banaaya ja rahaa he or ek helmet kii laagat qareeb 6500 rupee he
 Along with this, a senior officer says, "now we have started giving it to some of our troops
 " Earlier, the helmet that NSG commandos wore was not bulletproof due to which the splinter hit it and it injured the young men
 phir javaanon ne bulatopruf pataka pahananaa shuru kiya jisase uske sirf maathe kii hifaazat hoti thi sir kii nahin
 The comments rajesh negi ke saath bhi aisa hi hua tha
 When he got the news of the entry of terrorists into the Pathankot airbase, he along with his comrades were engaged in a search operation
 kareeb dhai hajaar kii aabaadi vaale living aria ke paas unka aamanaa-saamana aatankiyon se hua to unke saamne sabase badi chunauti logon kii jaan bachaana tha
 When his comrades challenged the terrorists, the attackers hurled grenades at him
 grenade fatate hi uske chharre rajesh ke sharir main ghus gaye
 Some of the shrapnel went into his eyes and he was injured
 haalanki is haalat main bhi unhone anya javaanon ke saath milakar do aatankiyon ko dher kar diya

 These helmets fulfill the global standard
 saath hi ye helmet pahanane main suvidhajanak hai or inamen sanchaar upkarnon ko bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 In this regard, a senior officer of NSG told NDTV India, "no matter how close the bullet is fired, if a soldier is wearing this helmet, then there will be no injury to his head
 is helmet main koi nat nahin he
 It weighs two and a half kilos
 " According to him, in any anti-terror operation, the body gear of commandos is about 28 kg
 ab usamen do kilo kaa or izaafaa ho jayega
 In this case, one of the commandos associated with such an anti-terror operation says, "it is very important that your head is protected
" jab goli chal rahi hoti he to wo kahin bhi hit kar sakati he
 Earlier we used to save our heads but now our safety has also increased with this helmet
 " The best thing is that it is being made in India itself and the cost of a helmet is around 6500 rupees
 iske saath hi ek varisht afasar kaa kahana he,"abhi hamane apni kuch tukadiyon ko ise dena shuru kiya he
 " isse pehle jo helmet enesji ke commando pahante the uskaa sheesha bulatopruf nahin tha jiske kaaran splinter lagane se wo chur ho jaataa tha or jawaano kii aankh main chot lag jaati thi
 Then the soldiers started wearing bulletproof slabs which protected only his forehead and not the head
 tippaniyan The same happened with Rajesh Negi

 The BJP has returned to power after the results of the Lok Sabha 2019 elections
 narendra modi kii aguai main lagaataar duusari baar purna bahumat kii sarkaar banane ja rahi he
 Saffron also waved in Karnataka
 bijepi ne rajya kii 28 loksabhaa siton main se 25 siton par jeet darj kii
 Most of the party's candidates won by a margin of 1-2 lakhs
 mallikarjun khadge ke alaava kai congress netaaon ke haarane ke baad bijepi pradesh adhyaksh bies yediurppa ne jamkar tanj ksaa
 He said, "people have taught a lesson to those who speak against PM Modi
" yah pehali baar he jab karnataka main gaiyr-congress party ne itani siten jiti hai
 As soon as BJP seats started increasing, fireworks started and sweets were distributed outside the party office in Malleswaram
 yediurppa ne kaha ki jaisaa bhedbhaav rajya kii gathbandhan sarkaar (congress-jedies) ne dikhaaya, log use bardaasht nahin karenge
 However, Yeddyurappa did not reveal what his party plans to do next
 yediurppa ke sahyogi or purv dipti siem aar ashok ne india today ko bataaya ki yah karnataka kii janata ne yediurppa ke liye janadesh diya he
 He said, at this time CM HD Kumaraswamy should resign and hold elections again
 is baat par yediurppa ke bete biwai vijendra bhi sahamat najar aae
 He said that the mandate of the people of Karnataka is clear that he is fed up with the coalition government and he wants to see BJP in power again
